### [214] [Recovery of Planted Subgraphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00897)
*Wasim Huleihel*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了在稠密Erdős–Rényi随机图中精确恢复任意种植被子图的问题，提出了以"最小最大子图密度"为核心的统计阈值，并分析了多项式时间算法的性能与计算复杂度下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作大多局限于团、双团或稠密块等特殊子图族，对于一般种植子图在随机图中的精确恢复问题理解不足。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立通用框架。

Method: 1) 引入新图论量"最小最大子图密度"刻画精确恢复的统计阈值；2) 建立匹配的上界与下界，证明条件的最优性；3) 提出基于邻接矩阵谱性质的多项式时间恢复算法；4) 利用低次多项式框架推导计算下界；5) 扩展到半随机模型和更弱的恢复概念。

Result: 给出了任意种植子图精确恢复的尖锐充分必要条件；提出了适用于任意子图的计算高效算法；划定了统计可能但计算困难的区域。

Conclusion: 本文为一般种植子图的精确恢复问题提供了完整的统计与计算刻画，揭示了"最小最大子图密度"作为核心量的作用，并为未来在更复杂模型下的研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Understanding the fundamental limits of recovering planted subgraphs in random graphs is a central challenge in high-dimensional statistics and theoretical computer science. While existing work has largely focused on special subgraph families such as cliques, bicliques, or dense blocks, the exact recovery of a general planted subgraph in Erdős--Rényi random graphs remains poorly understood. In this paper, we study the exact recovery of an arbitrary planted subgraph $Γ= Γ_n$ embedded in a dense Erdős--Rényi random graph $\mathcal{G}(n,q_n)$, where edges within $Γ$ are present independently with probability $p_n > q_n$.
  Our main results identify sharp conditions under which exact recovery is possible with high probability, and we establish matching lower bounds showing the necessity of these conditions. The resulting statistical threshold is characterized by a new graph-theoretic quantity, which we term the \emph{minimal maximum subgraph density}. This quantity is defined as the maximum subgraph density of the smallest induced balanced subgraph of $Γ$.
  We then turn to the problem of recovery under polynomial-time constraints. We propose a computationally efficient recovery algorithm that applies to arbitrary planted subgraphs and analyze its performance in terms of certain spectral properties of the adjacency matrix. In addition, we derive computational lower bounds for recovery using the low-degree polynomial framework, establishing regimes where recovery is statistically possible but computationally hard. Finally, we consider several extensions of our setting, including recovery in semi-random models and weaker notions of recovery.

</details>


### [215] [Fundamental Limits of Random Downlink Integrated Sensing and Communication over Rician Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00912)
*Marziyeh Soltani,Mahtab Mirmohseni,Rahim Tafazolli,Mark F. Flanagan*

TL;DR: 本文研究了Rician衰落信道下下行MIMO ISAC系统的随机性能，分析了两种波束赋形策略（SJB和LB）的通信和感知中断概率，揭示了Rician K因子对通信影响更大且呈现非单调行为，以及不同波束赋形策略在不同环境下的性能权衡。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多基于瑞利衰落假设，而实际LoS主导场景中确定性传播分量会显著影响感知和通信可靠性，特别是角度相关性使得随机向量独立但非同分布，需要新的分析框架。

Method: 针对SJB（共享波形最优）和LB（实用线性波束赋形）两种策略，基于CRB推导通信中断概率和感知中断概率，分析大系统和高峰值功率缩放律，并推导LB的上下界及可处理近似。

Result: Rician K因子对通信性能影响强于感知，具有非单调行为；高功率下LB无DPC受雷达自干扰限制；LB+DPC在强LoS环境最优且是瑞利衰落中唯一实现超高通信可靠性的方案；SJB是低复杂度的鲁棒替代方案。

Conclusion: 不同波束赋形策略在不同信道条件和工作功率下各有优劣，需根据LoS强度、功率预算和复杂度约束选择合适方案。

Abstract: This paper studies the stochastic performance of a downlink multiple-input multiple-output integrated sensing and communication (ISAC) system over Rician fading channels. Rician fading is important in line-of-sight (LoS)-dominated deployments, where a deterministic propagation component can strongly affect sensing and communication reliability. The base station (BS) simultaneously serves a user and senses a target. The BS-user channel contains LoS and non-line-of-sight components. The user LoS angle may be fixed or random, and the target angle may follow an arbitrary distribution potentially correlated with the user angle. Compared with Rayleigh fading, the deterministic LoS component introduces angle-dependent terms and leads to generally independent but non-identically distributed random vectors, requiring new analysis.
  We analyze two beamforming strategies: subspace joint beamforming (SJB), optimal for the shared waveform structure, and linear beamforming (LB), a practical alternative using separate sensing and communication beamformers. For both schemes, we derive communication outage probability (OP) and sensing OP based on the Cramer--Rao bound (CRB). We also identify special cases with simpler expressions. For LB, we derive upper and lower bounds on sensing OP and a tractable approximation.
  We characterize large-system and high-power scaling laws. LB without dirty paper coding (DPC) is interference-limited at high power due to radar self-interference. Results show the Rician K-factor affects communication more strongly than sensing, with non-monotonic behavior across regimes. LB with DPC achieves the best overall performance in strong LoS environments and is the only scheme achieving ultra-high communication reliability in Rayleigh fading, while SJB provides a robust lower-complexity alternative across operating conditions.

</details>


### [216] [DRL-Based Joint Beamforming and Surface Shape Optimization for Flexible Intelligent Metasurface-Aided ISAC Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00951)
*Maoyuan Wang,Qian Zhang,Jiancheng An,Xuejun Cheng,Zheng Dong,Deqiang Wang*

TL;DR: 本文研究基于柔性智能超表面（FIM）的ISAC系统，通过深度强化学习（DDPG）联合优化波束赋形矩阵和FIM表面形状，在满足通信QoS约束下最小化克拉美罗界（CRB）。数值结果表明联合优化显著降低CRB并保证通信质量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将波束赋形矩阵与FIM表面形状的联合设计建模为CRB最小化问题，并施加发射功率、QoS和FIM形状约束；针对非凸难解特性，采用深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）演员-评论家DRL框架，设计约束感知奖励函数引导策略学习。

Result: 与现有刚性阵列相比，联合优化波束赋形矩阵和FIM表面形状能够显著降低CRB（即提升感知精度），同时保证通信服务质量满足约束。

Conclusion: 柔性智能超表面结合DRL优化是提升ISAC系统感知性能的有效途径，为未来灵活可重构的感知-通信一体化设计提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Integrated sensing and communication (ISAC) unifies high-precision sensing and wireless data transmission. In this paper, we investigate the design of ISAC systems enabled by flexible intelligent metasurface (FIM) and aim to minimize the Cramér-Rao bound (CRB) with quality of service (QoS) constraints using deep reinforcement learning (DRL). Specifically, we formulate the joint design of beamforming matrix and FIMs surface shape to reduce the CRB subject to transmit power, QoS and the FIMs surface shape constraints. However, the non-convex formulation makes optimization problem difficult to solve. To tackle this issue, we develop a deep deterministic policy gradient (DDPG) actor critic DRL scheme for the joint design, guided by a constraint aware reward to progressively improve sensing performance. Numerical results demonstrate that jointly optimizing the beamforming matrix and the FIMs surface shape substantially decreases CRB while ensuring communication quality compared with existing rigid arrays.

### [217] [QuaMoE-DRF: Proactive Beam and Rate Adaptation via Multimodal Dynamic Radio Map Forecasting in ISAC Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00974)
*Zhihan Zeng,Kaihe Wang,Zhongpei Zhang,Chongwen Huang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出QuaMoE-DRF，一种面向ISAC网络的质量感知多模态动态无线电地图预测框架，通过预测未来波束-SINR场实现主动波束和速率自适应。融合静态几何、运动观测、感知状态和无线历史数据，采用质量感知的混合专家模块处理异构模态误差，联合预测通信导向的信道地图及主动BS/波束/MCS决策。在动态多BS多UE城区基准上达到402.5Mbps有效速率、0.0417中断概率、0.1836地图RMSE，有效速率提升5.67%，中断降低8.35%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态无线电地图无法捕获移动物体造成的短时遮挡；直接传感辅助波束预测因波束索引丢弃了SINR余量、MCS阈值、BS备选及通信等效邻波束等信息，存在局限性。

Method: 提出质量感知多模态动态无线电地图预测框架（QuaMoE-DRF），核心表征为未来波束-SINR场；证明完整多BS波束-SINR场对有限码本阈值率决策充分；为可解性，学习紧凑参考BS局部场，辅以BS级监督、联合BS-波束监督及潜在网络上下文；融合静态几何、类事件运动观测、结构化感知状态及无线历史，通过质量感知混合专家模块（基于异质模态误差下的逆方差融合）进行预测。

Result: 在动态多BS多UE城区基准上，有效速率402.5 Mbps，中断概率0.0417，地图RMSE 0.1836；相比最强有效速率基线，有效速率提升5.67%，中断降低8.35%。

Conclusion: QuaMoE-DRF通过质量感知多模态融合和波束-SINR场预测，有效提升了ISAC网络中主动波束与速率自适应的性能，验证了该框架的有效性和优越性。

Abstract: Static radio maps provide location-dependent propagation priors, but they cannot capture short-term blockage caused by moving objects. Direct sensing-assisted beam prediction is also limited because a beam index discards SINR margins, MCS thresholds, BS alternatives, and communication-equivalent neighboring beams. This paper proposes QuaMoE-DRF, a quality-aware multimodal dynamic radio map forecasting framework for proactive beam and rate adaptation in ISAC networks. Its core representation is a future beam-SINR field. We show that the full multi-BS beam-SINR field is sufficient for finite-codebook threshold-rate BS, beam, MCS, goodput, and outage decisions. For tractability, the implemented model learns a compact reference-BS local field, complemented by BS-level supervision, joint BS--beam supervision, and latent network context; we also clarify that this compact projection alone is not sufficient for BS association. QuaMoE-DRF fuses static geometry, event-like motion observations, structured sensing states, and wireless history through a quality-aware mixture-of-experts module motivated by inverse-variance fusion under heteroscedastic modality errors. It jointly predicts communication-oriented map channels and proactive BS, beam, and MCS decisions. On a dynamic multi-BS and multi-UE urban benchmark, QuaMoE-DRF achieves 402.5 Mbps effective rate, 0.0417 outage probability, and 0.1836 map RMSE, improving the effective rate by 5.67% and reducing outage by 8.35% over the strongest completed effective-rate baseline. The current validation uses labels from a compact blockage/path-loss simulator, with ray tracing used only for calibration and sanity checking.

### [218] [From Welfare to Utility: Generalized Objectives in Budget-Feasible Procurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00101)
*Alon Eden,Eldar Kerner,Kira Goldner,Thodoris Tsilivis*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究预算约束采购问题中的机制设计，在买家有预算限制的情况下，设计了近似最优的买家效用、社会福利等目标机制，包括无先验环境下的福利近似机制和贝叶斯环境下的效用最优机制，并推广到其他目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作主要关注买家价值最大化，而本文旨在求解买家效用（价值减支付）、社会福利（价值减生产成本）及其推广目标下的最优或近似最优机制，填补了这些目标下机制设计的空白。

Method: 对于社会福利目标，设计了无先验（最坏情况）下的常数因子近似机制。对于买家效用目标，由于无先验机制无法提供任何保证，转向贝叶斯设定，先设计了满足期望预算约束的效用最优机制，再修改为满足事后（ex-post）预算约束的近似最优机制，并推广到其他目标。

Result: 社会福利目标下获得了常数因子近似机制；买家效用目标下在贝叶斯设定中获得了最优及近似最优机制，且能保证事后预算约束；机制可推广至其他广义目标。

Conclusion: 本文为预算约束采购问题提供了不同目标下的最优或近似最优机制设计，拓展了该问题的理论边界，尤其在买家效用和社会福利目标上取得了实质性进展。

Abstract: We study mechanism design for the budget-feasible procurement problem, a natural problem that arises when a buyer wants to procure goods or services from multiple strategic sellers who each have a cost to provide that service, the buyer has a value for each service procured, but is constrained by a budget. In contrast to prior work, which has focused on buyer value maximization for this problem, we solve for optimal and approximately-optimal mechanisms for the objectives of buyer utility (value of procured services minus payments), welfare (value minus production costs), and generalizations of the two. For welfare, we design a simple mechanism that obtains a constant-factor approximation for the prior-free (worst-case) setting. As prior-free mechanisms fail to provide any guarantee for utility, even for a single seller, we consider Bayesian settings, where the buyer has distributional knowledge over sellers' costs. We first provide a utility-optimal mechanism that satisfies the buyer's budget constraint in expectation, then we show how to modify the mechanism to satisfy the budget constraint ex-post, for every realization of seller costs, while still obtaining near-optimal utility guarantees. Finally, we generalize our mechanisms to other objectives.

### [219] [Data Sharing and Competition in Learning-by-Deploying Industries: Insights from Robotics and Beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00168)
*Yunjin Tong,Luca-Andrei Manea*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究“部署中学习”（Learning-by-Deploying）——即产品部署产生的数据驱动下一代技术改进——在竞争性市场中如何与企业的部署决策及产品市场竞争相互作用，发现当企业间共享学习数据（即池化）时，下游竞争会降低共享的私人价值，甚至可能使其为负。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多现代技术（如AI、自动驾驶等）通过部署使用产生数据来改进自身，这意味着部署不仅是生产，更是对共享学习存量的投资。然而，这种学习的架构（企业间池化共享 vs. 企业内碎片化）如何影响企业的部署决策及市场竞争，现有文献尚缺乏系统研究。

Method: 构建一个两期模型，对称企业做出不可逆的产能选择，产能使用产生的数据驱动学习曲线，提升未来生产率。分别在外生价格和下游古诺（Cournot）竞争两种市场结构下，分析学习数据池化（pooling）与碎片化（fragmentation）对部署决策、社会福利及企业私人激励的影响。

Result: 外生价格下，数据池化提升社会福利，但企业会低投早期部署；引入下游古诺竞争后，池化降低市场价格，使得共享数据的私人价值随竞争加剧而下降，甚至可能转为负值。研究还刻画了一个可持续性阈值，该阈值由池化所诱导产出范围内的行业需求弹性决定，并通过数值分析验证了相关模式。

Conclusion: 数据共享的福利效应依赖于市场竞争结构：垄断或外生定价时共享有益，但竞争环境下共享可能损害企业私人激励。政策制定需关注行业需求弹性等条件，以避免共享机制在竞争市场中不可持续。

Abstract: Many modern technologies improve through use. Each unit deployed generates data that trains the next generation, so deployment is both production and an investment in a shared learning stock. We study how the architecture of this learning, whether pooled across firms or fragmented within them, interacts with firms' deployment decisions and with product-market competition. In a two-period model, symmetric firms make irreversible capacity choices, and capacity in use feeds a learning curve that raises future productivity. We call this learning-by-deploying, replacing the production experience of the classic learning-by-doing tradition with deployment-generated data. With exogenous prices, pooling raises welfare but firms underinvest in early deployment. Downstream Cournot competition overturns this: pooling depresses the price, so the private value of sharing falls with competition and can turn negative. We characterize a sustainability threshold governed, under general demand, by the elasticity of industry demand over the output range pooling induces, and confirm the patterns numerically.

### [220] [Knowing Who, Not How Much: Learning-Augmented Mechanisms for Consumer Utility Maximization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00175)
*Kira Goldner,Divyarthi Mohan,Thodoris Tsilivis*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 研究在线随机顺序模型中战略Agent的消费者效用最大化问题。通过引入学习增强机制设计框架，发现传统预测（如Agent价值或最优价值）无效，而最高价值Agent的身份预测有效。提出确定性真话机制，并利用预测实现常数近似的最优解（正确预测时）和常数近似的最佳可实现解（错误预测时）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线随机顺序模型中，战略Agent的消费者效用最大化面临强不可能性结果，传统机制设计方法无法解决，因此借助学习增强机制设计框架寻求突破。

Method: 首先调整离线随机化技术，设计适用于在线环境的确定性真话机制；然后引入最高价值Agent身份预测来增强机制，分别分析预测正确（一致性）和错误（鲁棒性）时的性能保证。

Result: 预测正确时，机制实现常数近似于完全信息下的最优解（一致性）；预测任意错误时，仍保证常数近似于最佳可实现解（鲁棒性）。

Conclusion: 学习增强机制设计中，预测类型的选择至关重要。对于消费者效用最大化问题，最高价值Agent身份预测而非价值预测是有效的替代方案，能在一致性和鲁棒性之间取得平衡。

Abstract: We study consumer utility maximization in an online random-order model where strategic agents arrive sequentially. To circumvent strong impossibility results for utility maximization, we turn to the framework of learning-augmented mechanism design. Crucially, we show that the types of predictions commonly used in learning-augmented mechanism design (such as predictions of agent values or the optimal value) are not useful for utility maximization, where payments are directly at odds with the objective. Instead, we identify that a qualitatively different kind of prediction suffices: the identity of the highest-valued agent. First, we provide a deterministic truthful mechanism for our online setting by adapting offline randomized techniques. Then, we augment our mechanism with predictions. When the predictions are correct, we achieve a constant approximation to the optimal solution under full information (consistency), and even when predictions are arbitrarily bad, we guarantee a constant approximation to the best implementable solution (robustness).

### [221] [Fully Distributed Tâtonnement for Chores Markets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00300)
*Bhaskar Ray Chaudhury,Christian Kroer,Ruta Mehta,Tianlong Nan*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为"乘法试错法"的完全分布式价格调整动力学，用于解决带有苦役的Fisher市场中的竞争均衡计算问题。该方法仅依赖每个苦役自身的超额需求信号更新价格，无需全局耦合，并证明了其收敛性，实验表明该方法在实践中比已有的相对试错法快一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有用于苦役市场的相对试错法虽然恢复了收敛性，但代价是价格更新在所有苦役之间耦合（全局耦合），而能否通过真正局部的、仅依赖自身超额需求信号的更新来恢复收敛性，是一个悬而未决的问题。

Method: 乘法试错法：每个苦役的价格仅使用其当前价格和自身的超额需求信号进行更新。更新中没有显式的归一化项，但利用瓦尔拉斯定律和乘性更新的形式隐式地保持了相关的总体价格几何结构。

Result: 证明了在具有连续、凸且1-齐次（CCH）负效用的任意苦役Fisher市场中，乘法试错法收敛到竞争均衡。对于凸CES负效用，进一步证明了近似竞争均衡的收敛率与相对试错法相同（O(1/ε²)），但在问题常数上的依赖性更优。实验表明该方法在实践中比相对试错法快约一个数量级。

Conclusion: 乘法试错法是一种有效的、完全分布式的苦役市场均衡计算动力学，解决了全局耦合问题，并且在理论和实践中都表现出更好的性能。

Abstract: We study price-adjustment dynamics for computing competitive equilibria (CE) in Fisher markets with chores. Unlike in classical goods markets, prices in chores markets are payments for taking on undesirable tasks, and natural excess-demand dynamics can fail; even the naïve analogue of Walrasian tâtonnement may diverge. Recent work of Chaudhury et al. [2025] overcomes this obstacle via relative tâtonnement, which subtracts the average excess-demand signal from the excess demand vector. This recovers convergence, but at the cost of coupling the price updates across all chores. This leaves open whether such global coupling is inherent, or whether convergent tâtonnement can be recovered through a genuinely local update in which each chore reacts only to its own excess demand.
  We answer this question affirmatively through multiplicative tâtonnement, a fully distributed dynamics in which each chore price is updated using only its current price and its own excess-demand signal. Although the update contains no explicit normalization term, Walras' law and the multiplicative form of the update implicitly preserve the relevant aggregate price geometry. We prove that multiplicative tâtonnement converges to a CE in any chores Fisher market with continuous, convex, and $1$-homogeneous (CCH) disutilities. For convex CES disutilities, we further prove an approximate-CE convergence rate with the same $O(1/\varepsilon^2)$ dependence as relative tâtonnement, but with improved dependence on problem constants. Experiments on real-world and simulated instances show that multiplicative tâtonnement is substantially faster in practice, often by an order of magnitude.

</details>


### [222] [Positive and Negative Determinant Strategies in Repeated Games with Behavior-Value Inconsistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00625)
*Yuan Liu,Yakun Wang,Bin Wu*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种考虑行为与内心价值不一致成本的新博弈框架，证明了在此条件下零行列式（ZD）策略不存在，取而代之发现了一类新的正/负行列式策略，能够实现单方面收益控制，且控制能力优于经典ZD策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典直接互惠和ZD策略研究忽略了智能体行为与内心想法不一致所产生的内部成本，而这种不一致对决策至关重要，因此需要建立考虑内部成本的新理论框架。

Method: 建立博弈论框架，假设个体在行为与内心想法不一致时需支付内部成本；在重复囚徒困境中分析存在该成本时的策略空间，证明ZD策略不存在并推导出新的正/负行列式策略。

Result: （1）存在行为-价值不一致成本时，经典ZD策略不存在；（2）发现了正/负行列式策略，可强制两个个体平均收益的仿射组合大于/小于零；（3）负行列式策略可单方面控制对手收益低于给定值，正行列式策略可使焦点个体获得比对手更高的收益；（4）新策略的控制能力优于经典ZD策略。

Conclusion: 行为与价值之间的不一致对收益控制有重要影响，这一因素是经典ZD策略所缺失的，引入内部成本的新框架拓展了重复博弈中单向收益控制的理论。

Abstract: Direct reciprocity, based on the repeated interactions, is a fundamental mechanism to promote cooperation. Zero-determinant (ZD) strategies have opened an avenue for unilateral payoff control. However, previous studies neglect internal costs provided what agents do differ from what agents think, which is crucial for decision making of intelligent agents. Motivated by this, we establish a game theoretical framework by assuming that an individual pays the internal cost if the behavior is inconsistent with the internal thought. We prove that ZD strategy does not exist if the cost via behavior-value inconsistency is present. Instead, we find a new class of repeated strategies that enforce a unilateral payoff control, which is termed as positive/negative determinant strategy. The found strategy allows an individual to enforce an affine combination of two individuals' average payoffs above/below zero. Consequently, a focal individual is able to unilaterally control the opponent's payoff below a given value via negative determinant strategy, and a focal individual is able to get more payoff than the opponent via positive determinant strategy. We also find that the control ability of positive/negative determinant strategies is better off than that of ZD strategies. Our work highlights the importance of inconsistency between the behavior and value on payoff control, which is typically absent in classic ZD strategies.

</details>


### [223] [Which Voting Rules Are More Resilient to Coalitional Manipulation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00758)
*François Durand*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文通过一个极简模型（仅捕捉某一偏好排名相对其他排名的优势程度）系统分析了所有标准序数投票规则在扰动文化模型下对联盟操纵的鲁棒性。研究发现每种规则都存在尖锐的相变阈值，并据此识别出三类规则家族（基于不同强度的Condorcet胜者概念），该模型在真实数据集上能准确预测规则的相对脆弱性及其随候选人数的变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究哪些投票规则对联盟操纵更具鲁棒性，并寻找能够预测规则相对脆弱性的极简模型。

Method: 采用扰动文化模型（Impartial Culture的变体，通过额外权重参数化某一排名），系统分析所有标准序数投票规则在该模型下的表现，识别相变阈值并据此对规则进行分组。

Result: 每种规则展现出尖锐的相变现象；Maximin、Ranked Pairs、Schulze、Young共享相同阈值（第一类）；Baldwin、Nanson、Kemeny、Dodgson形成另一类；Black、Slater、Copeland构成第三类。在Netflix和FairVote真实数据集上，模型准确预测了规则的相对脆弱性及其随候选人数的演化趋势。

Conclusion: 一个极简的、无需调参的模型能够有效捕捉投票规则的比较脆弱性，规则的选择主要取决于候选人数目。

Abstract: Which voting rules are more resilient to coalitional manipulation? We find that a deliberately minimal model, capturing only the degree of advantage of one preference ranking over the others, can predict their relative vulnerability remarkably well.  Extending prior work on three rules, we systematically analyze all standard ordinal voting rules under the Perturbed Culture model, a variant of Impartial Culture parameterized by the extra weight assigned to one ranking. Each rule exhibits a sharp phase transition: manipulation succeeds with high probability below a critical concentration threshold, and fails above it. This structure reveals natural families of rules: seemingly distinct methods such as Maximin, Ranked Pairs, Schulze, and Young share identical thresholds, while Baldwin, Nanson, Kemeny, and Dodgson form another. These groupings are driven by new, strengthened notions of Condorcet winners. In addition, we identify a third family based on a previously introduced Condorcet notion: Black, Slater, and Copeland.  Empirically, the model displays strong predictive power. Tested on real-world datasets (Netflix and FairVote), it accurately ranks rules by vulnerability, predicts how this ranking evolves with the number of candidates, and explains why empirically similar clusters persist despite large absolute differences in manipulation rates, with a more nuanced picture for Bucklin and veto-based rules. Thus, an extremely parsimonious model with no tuning captures the comparative vulnerability of voting rules: which rules to prefer depends largely on the number of candidates alone.

</details>


### [224] [Multiwinner Voting with Spatial Preferences under Incomplete Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01036)
*Drew Springham,Edith Elkind,Bart de Keijzer,Maria Polukarov*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究在选民无法评估所有候选人的多赢家选举中，如何通过少量平面查询（Planar queries）实现强比例公平（EJR+）。在轴对齐随机矩形选民（ARRV）空间模型下，提出一种算法，仅需每选民期望O(d log dk)次查询即可返回EJR+委员会，查询次数与候选人数m无关，而是取决于议题数d和委员会规模k。算法核心是一个维度无关的验证或回退框架，并提供了针对已知、未知和平滑分布的模块。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在参与式预算或大规模推荐等多赢家选举中，候选人数量庞大，选民无法评估所有候选人。然而，标准的比例公平保证（如EJR+）要求选民提供完整的审批选票，这在现实中不切实际。本文旨在探讨能否在仅从每位选民获取少量信息的情况下，仍然保证强比例代表性。

Method: 采用ARRV空间模型（候选人在d维议题空间，选民审批轴对齐超矩形），通过平面查询（每查询比较选民对某个议题的容忍度与候选人在该议题的位置）获取偏好。提出一个维度无关的验证或回退（verify-or-fallback）框架，其查询成本由两个可互换模块的属性决定。针对已知分布、未知分布和平滑分布分别设计了相应模块。

Result: 算法在选民数量足够大时，每选民期望查询次数为O(d log dk)，与候选人数量m无关。该算法能在ARRV模型下对任意矩形偏好分布返回满足EJR+的委员会。三种设置（已知分布、未知分布、平滑分布）下均实现了端到端的保证。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在空间偏好模型下，通过精心设计的查询策略，可以用远少于完整审批选票的信息实现强比例公平，查询复杂度仅依赖于议题维度和委员会规模，而非候选人数。这为大规模多赢家选举中的偏好 elicitation 提供了理论可行的方案。

Abstract: In multiwinner elections with many candidates, as in participatory budgeting or large-scale recommendation, voters cannot plausibly evaluate every candidate, yet standard proportional-fairness guarantees such as EJR+ are stated for fully specified approval ballots. We ask whether strong proportional representation can still be guaranteed while eliciting only a little from each voter. We study this in a spatial model, the Axis-aligned Random Rectangle Voter (ARRV) model, in which candidates occupy a $d$-dimensional issue space and each voter approves an axis-aligned hyper-rectangle: a tolerance interval on every issue. Preferences are revealed only through Planar queries, each comparing a voter's tolerance to a candidate on a single issue. We give an algorithm returning an EJR+ committee for any distribution over rectangular preferences, using only $\mathcal{O}(d\log dk)$ Planar queries per voter in expectation given a sufficiently large electorate, independent of the number of candidates $m$, where $d$ is the number of issues and $k$ the committee size. The algorithm rests on a dimension-agnostic verify-or-fallback framework whose query cost is governed by two properties supplied by interchangeable modules. We describe such modules, yielding end-to-end guarantees for known, unknown, and smooth distributions.

</details>


### [225] [Fair Allocation under Conflict Constraints via Strong Colorability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01059)
*Ishay Haviv*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究冲突约束下的公平分配问题，引入强色数层次结构，揭示了公平分配与图论参数之间的紧密联系。针对SD-EF1给出了完全特征化，针对EF1和EF[1,1]给出了充分条件，并证明了最大度为Δ的图在至少3Δ-1个代理时存在公平分配，进一步给出了确定性的多项式时间算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究冲突约束（图中相邻顶点不能分配给同一代理）下的公平分配问题，针对代理具有共同偏好的场景，从三个公平性准则（SD-EF1、EF1、EF[1,1]）出发进行系统分析。

Method: 引入强色数（strong chromatic number）的变体层次结构，建立公平分配问题与图论参数之间的统一关联框架。通过图论方法分析不同公平准则下所需代理数量的充分必要条件。

Result: (1) 对SD-EF1完全刻画了保证公平分配所需代理数量；(2) 对EF1和EF[1,1]给出了充分条件，并证明其并非必要条件；(3) 最大度为Δ的图在至少3Δ-1个代理时均存在SD-EF1、EF1和EF[1,1]分配；(4) 提供确定性多项式时间算法，当代理数至少为(3+ε)Δ时可在多项式时间内找到公平分配。

Conclusion: 本文建立的强色数层次结构为冲突约束下的公平分配提供了统一的理论框架，不仅在存在性上给出了紧的或充分的界，还带来了算法上的进展，强化了Barman和Viswanathan关于公平着色的已有工作。

Abstract: In the fair allocation problem under conflict constraints, the goal is to partition the vertices of a graph among agents in a fair manner, such that no two adjacent vertices are assigned to the same agent. We study this problem for agents with common preferences through the lens of three fairness criteria: stochastic-dominance envy-freeness up to one item for preference orders (SD-EF1), envy-freeness up to one item for monotone additive valuations (EF1), and envy-freeness up to one item from each side for general additive valuations (EF[1,1]). To do so, we introduce a hierarchy of variants of the strong chromatic number, a graph quantity introduced independently by Alon and Fellows in the early nineties. Our results reveal a close connection between fair allocation under conflict constraints and the first two levels of this hierarchy, providing a unified route to both existential and algorithmic results.
  For SD-EF1, we fully characterize the number of agents needed to guarantee a fair allocation of a given graph for every common preference order. For EF1 and EF[1,1], we provide analogous sufficient conditions, extending a result on path graphs due to Equbal, Gurjar, Igarashi, Kumar, Manurangsi, Nath, Saxena, Vaish, and Yoneda. We also show that, unlike in the SD-EF1 setting, the sufficient conditions for EF1 and EF[1,1] are not necessary in general. Our framework yields existential and algorithmic consequences in terms of the maximum degree. We obtain that every graph with maximum degree $Δ$ admits SD-EF1, EF1, and EF[1,1] allocations for common preferences whenever the number of agents is at least $3Δ-1$. We further provide, for any $\varepsilon>0$, deterministic polynomial-time algorithms that find such allocations whenever the number of agents is at least $(3+\varepsilon)Δ$. These guarantees strengthen earlier work by Barman and Viswanathan on equitable colorings.

</details>


### [226] [Online Fair Division Meets Reordering Buffers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01159)
*Georgios Amanatidis,Giulio Giaconi,Evangelos Markakis,Nicos Protopapas*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究在线公平分配不可分割混合甘露（物品价值可正可负）的问题，通过在算法中引入有限大小的缓冲区来存储和重排物品，在个性化k值实例上实现了每步EF1和大部分时间EF的分配，缓冲区大小与k和智能体数量呈线性关系，并将结果推广到一般加性估值函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线公平分配中，当物品价值可正可负（混合甘露）时，现有研究在没有额外假设的情况下存在强负面结果和稀缺的正面结果。本文旨在通过引入有限大小的缓冲区这一自然中间方案，在在线和离线场景之间建立桥梁，从而实现在线公平分配的可满足性。

Method: 本文采用带缓冲区的在线算法设计方法：1）缓冲区可以存储和重排有限数量的物品；2）针对个性化k值实例（每个智能体对物品最多有k种不同估值），构建线性于k和智能体数量的缓冲区；3）通过新颖的组合论证，构造一系列无嫉妒匹配来分配大部分物品；4）将结果扩展到一般加性估值函数，依赖同号取值间的最大比值；5）同时给出缓冲区尺寸更小情况下的不可能性结果。

Result: 1）在个性化k值实例中，使用大小为O(k·n)的缓冲区即可实现每步EF1且大多数时间步EF的分配；2）结果可推广到一般加性估值函数，但依赖于智能体同号值之间的最大比值；3）证明了缓冲区尺寸更小时的不可能性结果，揭示了方法的局限性。

Conclusion: 有限大小的缓冲区可以有效桥接在线与离线公平分配之间的鸿沟，在混合甘露场景下实现强公平性保证。缓冲区大小与参数k和智能体数量呈线性关系，且不能无限制缩小。

Abstract: We study the online fair division of indivisible mixed manna among agents with additive valuation functions. Under the standard online model, at each time step an indivisible item arrives; each agent may assign it a positive, negative, or zero value, and it must be irrevocably allocated, before the arrival of the next item. At the same time, we also wish to maintain some fairness guarantee, and in this work we focus on envy-freeness (EF) and one of its most prominent relaxations, envy-freeness up to one item (EF1). Given the strong negative and the scarce positive results for this problem without additional assumptions, we augment our algorithms with buffers that can store and rearrange a limited number of items. This setting interpolates naturally between the fully online case (no buffer) and the fully offline case (a buffer large enough to hold all items). We show that algorithms equipped with reasonably sized buffers can achieve strong guarantees for personalized $k$-value instances, i.e., instances in which each agent assigns at most $k$ distinct values to items. In particular, we construct allocations that are EF1 at every time step and EF at most time steps, using a buffer of size linear in $k$ and in the number of agents. Our approach relies on novel combinatorial arguments and on constructing a sequence of envy-free matchings that allocates most items. Finally, we extend our results to general additive valuation functions, with a dependence on the largest per-agent ratio between two values of the same sign, and we also identify limitations of our approach via impossibility results on the use of buffers with smaller size.

</details>

### [227] [Geometric Shape Optimization for Limbless Locomotion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00524)
*Utpal Khanal,Avirup Mandal*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于微分几何的框架，使用傅里叶-切比雪夫多项式基表示细长软体（如蛇）的三维参数曲线，通过优化求解曲线与环境交互，并引入弯曲和扭转能量项确保物理合理性和非自交行为，最终通过插值驱动表面实现可视化。实验表明该方法在仿真质量和物理真实性上优于现有技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无肢可变形生物的 locomotion 仿真在计算机图形学、软体机器人和计算建模中仍是一个具有挑战性的问题，现有方法难以有效模拟细长软体的物理真实运动。

Method: 1) 使用傅里叶-切比雪夫多项式基将蛇形软体表示为三维参数曲线；2) 通过求解优化问题估算多项式系数，确定曲线与环境交互；3) 引入弯曲和扭转能量项确保物理合理且无自交行为；4) 通过插值驱动表面表示，实现类似蒙皮技术的可视化。

Result: 在多种复杂场景和参数设置下进行了评估，与最先进方法相比，该方法实现了更高的仿真质量并生成了更物理真实的运动。

Conclusion: 该微分几何框架能够有效建模细长软体（如蛇）的运动，在仿真质量和物理真实性方面优于现有方法，具有鲁棒性和通用性。

Abstract: The simulation of locomotion in limbless, deformable organisms remains a challenging problem across computer graphics, soft robotics, and computational modeling. In this work, we present a novel differential-geometric framework for modeling the motion of slender soft bodies, such as snakes. The body is represented as a three-dimensional parametric curve using a Fourier-Chebyshev polynomial basis. Motion is computed by solving an optimization problem that determines the interaction between the curve and its environment by estimating polynomial coefficients. To ensure physically plausible and non-self-intersecting behavior, bending and torsional energy terms are incorporated into the formulation. The resulting curve is then used to drive a surface representation via interpolation, enabling realistic visualization analogous to skinning techniques. We evaluate the proposed approach across a range of complex scenarios and parameter settings to demonstrate its robustness and versatility. Comparative analysis with state-of-the-art methods indicates that our approach achieves improved simulation quality and generates more physically realistic motion.

### [228] [Constructive Alignment: Governing Preference Dynamics in Human-AI Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00001)
*Max Kanwal,Caryn Tran*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出"建构性对齐"范式，将AI对齐问题从静态偏好满足重构为对人类偏好演化轨迹的控制问题，强调AI系统应调控而非迎合人类价值观的形成过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI对齐方法将人类偏好视为静态、固定的优化目标，但行为经济学、心理学等大量实证证据表明偏好是分层、动态且在与适应性技术交互中建构的。随着AI系统日益持久化、个性化和社交嵌入，它们正积极参与塑造人们的注意力、价值观和认同，这使静态偏好假设与实际情况严重脱节。

Method: 借鉴行为经济学、心理学和建构主义社会理论，将偏好建模为与AI系统交互下演化的分层状态变量；采用控制论框架形式化描述，其中系统动作和交互设计共同影响世界状态和人类评价状态；将对齐重新定义为对长期价值形成的治理问题。

Result: 提出了建构性对齐的五个核心约束：价值轨迹连贯性、反思性认可、认识论基础性、免受操纵的边界性、不确定性下的赋能性。将对齐问题的焦点从控制AI行为转移至调控AI如何影响人类偏好的演化。

Conclusion: 对齐的核心不在于控制AI行为本身，而在于规范AI系统如何影响人类偏好的长期演化过程，确保价值轨迹在动态交互中保持健康、自主和赋能的方向。

Abstract: Most approaches to AI alignment treat human preferences as fixed targets to be inferred and optimized. This assumption conflicts with extensive empirical evidence showing that preferences are layered, dynamic, and constructed through interaction--particularly with adaptive technologies. As AI systems become more persistent, personalized, and socially embedded, they increasingly participate in shaping what people attend to, value, and endorse over time. We introduce Constructive Alignment, a paradigm that reframes alignment as a control problem over evolving human preference trajectories rather than static preference satisfaction. Drawing on behavioral economics, psychology, and constructivist social theory, we model preferences as layered state variables that evolve under interaction with AI systems. We formalize this view using a control-theoretic framework in which system actions and interaction design jointly influence both world states and human evaluative states. We argue that alignment is not primarily about controlling AI behavior, but about regulating how AI systems influence the evolution of human preferences--ensuring that value trajectories remain coherent, reflectively endorsed, epistemically grounded, bounded against manipulation, and empowering under uncertainty. Alignment thus becomes a problem of governing long-term value formation rather than simply satisfying static preferences.

</details>


### [229] [Bounded Morality: Defining the Space of Moral Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00002)
*Max Kanwal,Caryn Tran,Patrick Mineault*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出"有界道德"形式化框架，将道德认知建模为有限代理在道德广度与深度间的计算权衡，而非固定伦理规则的执行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统道德认知模型将人类视为遵循固定伦理理论（义务论、后果论、美德伦理）的静态规则执行者，忽略了有限计算资源对道德推理的根本约束。

Method: 扩展赫伯特·西蒙的有界理性概念，沿道德广度（道德相关实体的范围）与道德深度（评估交互所需的推理整合）两个正交维度形式化道德情境，并推导有限资源下两维度间不可避免的权衡关系。

Result: 定义了可行道德计算空间，将不同伦理理论解释为适应不同需求模式的局部高效策略；提出了形式化的道德遗憾与道德进步概念。

Conclusion: 人工系统中的道德对齐取决于道德推理能力的扩展与分配，而非直接模仿人类判断。

Abstract: Moral cognition has traditionally been modeled as adherence to fixed ethical theories--deontology, consequentialism, virtue ethics--implemented as static rules or value functions. We propose Bounded Morality, a formal framework for analyzing the computational demands of moral problems faced by finite agents. Extending Herbert Simon's notion of bounded rationality, we formalize moral situations along two orthogonal dimensions: moral breadth, the scope of entities treated as morally relevant, and moral depth, the inferential integration required to evaluate their interactions. Limited resources impose an unavoidable tradeoff between these dimensions, defining a feasible space of moral computation. Within this space, ethical theories correspond to locally efficient strategies adapted to different demand regimes rather than competing accounts of moral truth. The framework yields a formal notion of moral regret and moral progress under constraint, and implies that moral alignment in artificial systems depends on the scaling and allocation of moral reasoning capacity rather than on direct imitation of human judgments.

</details>


### [230] [The MMM Data Model -- A Normative Specification for Knowledge Interoperability in a Decentralisable Knowledge Commons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00032)

Abstract: Many information systems are built around documents: self-contained units optimised for print production and linear reading. While effective for large-scale dissemination, the document-centric organisation constrains how knowledge can be structured, updated, shared, and reused. Formal approaches address some of these limitations but struggle to achieve widespread contribution and adoption due to their prioritisation of formal structure over other system properties such as human usability and scope. AI systems are reshaping document production, but without providing a unified portable alternative to traditional documents for humans' expression and exchange of knowledge. This paper presents MMM, a data model for knowledge documentation that emerged from the practical needs of interdisciplinary collaborative research, and positioned here within a comparative analysis of the design space of information systems. MMM combines a small set of normative constraints with the expressive freedom of free-text labels. It is designed for interoperability across disciplines, applications and deployments without requiring semantic convergence. A reference implementation and pilot deployment data demonstrate implementability and early usability.

### [231] [Making Failure Safe: A Constrained, Verifiable Agent Framework for Open-Web Data Collection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00035)
*Bo Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种约束性、可验证的框架，将LLM输出从自由代码转向类型化JSON采集器配置，结合六类型采集器分类法、模板约束、静态Airflow DAG执行、规则质量检查与结构化反馈修正。在138个任务上验证了框架的可行性，在80个独立验证任务上实现了零执行阶段LLM令牌消耗和最低运行时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出约束性、可验证的智能体框架，核心包括：(1) 六类型采集器分类法；(2) 模板与工具函数约束；(3) 静态Airflow DAG执行；(4) 基于规则的质量检查；(5) 结构化反馈修正。将LLM输出从自由形式代码转化为类型化JSON采集器配置。

Result: 138个任务上验证分类法支持基于描述的意图分类；80个独立验证任务上框架实现零执行阶段LLM令牌消耗、最低平均墙钟时间，以适度牺牲一次性质量换取可复用、确定性、可验证的执行路径。

Conclusion: 该框架为重复性定时采集提供了一个可复用、低成本、可验证的执行路径，适合反复的开放网络数据采集场景。

Abstract: LLMs and agents can generate web scrapers from natural-language requirements, but direct generation remains unreliable because of dependency errors, broken selectors, schema mismatches, and heterogeneous page structures. We propose a constrained, verifiable agent framework that shifts LLM output from free-form code to typed JSON collector configurations, combining a six-type collector taxonomy, template and utility-function constraints, static Airflow DAG execution, rule-based quality checking, and structured feedback correction. Experiments on 138 tasks show that the taxonomy supports description-based requirement typing, while confirming that stable instantiation requires completing source, field, and execution constraints beyond the initial description. On 80 independently source-verified tasks, the framework runs with zero execution-stage LLM tokens and the lowest average wall-clock time, trading moderate one-shot quality for a reusable, deterministic, and verifiable execution path suited to repeated scheduled collection. These results position the framework as a reusable, low-cost, and verifiable execution path for repeated open-web data collection.

*Yiyuan Zou,Wenying Lyu,Clark Borst*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对空中交通管理中路径规划算法与管制员实际需求脱节的问题，提出了一种面向航路管制、兼具可解释性与计算效率的无冲突路径规划算法。该算法整合三种基于意图的冲突检测方法，并在解空间框架下提出顶点搜索（SSPPV）和边搜索（SSPPE）两种变体。实验表明，SSPPV结合区域冲突检测性能最优，在MUAC Delta扇区场景中平均计算时间仅3.69毫秒。

This underscores the need for decision-support solutions that are inherently interpretable, computationally efficient, and explicitly designed for human use. Focusing on this design challenge, this study develops a conflict-free path-planning algorithm for en-route Air Traffic Control (ATC) designed to be compatible with two guiding considerations: (1) the interpretability and flexibility offered by solution-space displays, which motivate constructing an algorithm that exposes all feasible safe actions and accommodates shifting optimization goals; and (2) the decision logic controllers naturally apply when enforcing operational constraints, such as separation standards, maneuverability limits, waypoint minimization, and routing practicality. Centered on these principles, the algorithm integrates three intent-based conflict detection methods -- distance-based, time-interval-based, and zone-based -- within a solution-space framework to identify conflict-free paths in computationally efficient ways. Additionally, vertex-based and edge-based search nodes are proposed for solution space path planning (SSPP), resulting in two variants -- SSPPV and SSPPE, respectively, which are evaluated in terms of computational speed and solution quality. Empirical results show that SSPPV paired with zone-based conflict detection achieves the best performance, computing paths in 3.69 ms on average in operational-relevant scenarios based on the Delta sector of the Maastricht Upper Area Control Centre (MUAC) using a 5 nmi grid.

### [234] [A Contextual-Bandit Oversight Game with Two-Sided Informational Asymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00155)
*Yunjin Tong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究AI与人类之间存在双向私有信息时的运行时人类监督问题，建立了一个具有双方不对称信息的上下文赌博团队博弈模型，给出了团队最优和近视规则两种单轮刻画，揭示了二者之间的"可避免伤害区间"——即AI明知行动有害但近视人类因信任先验而拒绝监督的情况，并分析了重复交互中通过被动学习和主动信号动态解决该问题的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实中的自主机器人或软件代理在检查了人类监督者无法直接评估的情境后，会产生自然的信息不对称：人类私下知道自己的奖励函数，而AI私下知道其提议行动的质量。这种双向私有信息使得人类对AI的运行时监督面临根本性挑战，需要对此进行理论刻画。

Method: 在合作逆强化学习(CIRL)和监督博弈的基础上，引入具有双面不对称信息的上下文赌博团队博弈，采用play/ask/trust/oversee交互界面。通过赌博机结构去除物理状态转移，从而在完整POMDP框架下原本只能推测的问题上获得精确的单轮刻画。

Result: 给出了两种单轮刻画：团队最优和近视规则，二者之间的差距构成"可避免伤害区间"——在该区间内AI私下知道行动有害且需要关闭，但近视人类因信任先验而拒绝监督。证明了该差距是"不可信的监督沟通"的代价，并给出了通过被动学习和滞后一期的主动信号在重复轮次中动态解决的部分分析。

Conclusion: 双向私有信息条件下，近视人类的监督决策会产生系统性可避免的伤害，该伤害源于监督沟通的不可信性，但通过重复交互中的学习和信号传递可以得到缓解。

Abstract: We study runtime human oversight of an AI agent when private information runs in both directions: the human privately knows her reward function, while the AI privately knows the quality of the action it proposes. This is the kind of asymmetry that arises naturally when an autonomous robot or software agent has inspected a situation its human supervisor cannot directly assess. Building on Cooperative Inverse Reinforcement Learning (CIRL) and the Oversight Game, we introduce a contextual-bandit team game with two-sided asymmetric information and a play/ask/trust/oversee interface. The bandit structure removes physical state transitions and thereby yields exact one-shot characterizations that would remain conjectural in the full POMDP setting, though the common belief remains a dynamically controlled state across rounds. We give two one-shot characterizations, a team optimum and a behaviorally natural myopic rule, whose gap is a slab of avoidable harm: a region in which the AI privately knows the proposed action is harmful and shutdown would help, yet a myopic human, trusting her prior, declines to oversee. We show this gap is the price of non-credible oversight communication, and give a partial analysis of how it resolves dynamically over repeated rounds through passive learning and active signaling with a one-period-lagged oversight response.

Drawing on the AIR (epistemic aims, ideals and reliable epistemic processes) framework, this study examines how epistemic aims and epistemic processes are enacted in GenAI-supported co-programming activities and explores scalable approaches for operationalizing these constructs in interaction data. Using a large dialogue dataset of human-AI co-programming, this study identifies observable dimensions of epistemic aims (i.e., mastery-oriented aims) and epistemic processes (i.e., outsourcing, explanation seeking, verification seeking, prompt monitoring, and epistemic justification). The results reveal a prevalent lack of EAIL, with 78.8% of student-GenAI interactions relying on non-mastery-oriented aims and less reliable epistemic strategies like outsourcing and verification-seeking. Conversely, only 11.1% of interactions showed high epistemic engagement, where mastery-oriented aims were coupled with advanced epistemic strategies like epistemic justification in a more reliable epistemic process.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: How do two agents invent a shared language from scratch? In a Lewis signaling game, a sender and receiver must coordinate on a code using only their interaction history. We study five memory architectures across varying channel configurations with LLM agents and find that memory architecture matters more than channel capacity. Agents with a persistent private notebook benefit from surplus channel capacity and avoid the high-capacity collapse seen in stateless agents, achieving the most reliable coordination ($0.867 \pm 0.023$ at capacity = 25). Stateless agents peak at moderate capacity and then degrade as the vocabulary grows beyond what a rolling context window can track The notebook externalizes learned conventions, freeing agents from having to re-derive codes each round. An information bottleneck-inspired argument predicts an optimal capacity equal to the number of objects. Instead, the bottleneck (capacity = 8) proves to be a fragility point, and surplus capacity is generally better. We show that channel capacity alone cannot predict coordination; memory architecture determines whether agents turn interaction history into stable conventions, and both dimensions are needed to understand how signals become language.

### [238] [Mnemosyne: Agentic Transaction Processing for Validating and Repairing AI-generated Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00269)
*Edward Y. Chang,Longling Geng,Emily J. Chang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Agentic事务处理（ATP）模型，将生成的动作视为不可信提案，通过运行时确定性准入和约束集C保证提交状态正确性，并在Mnemosyne系统中实现，证明四项安全属性且开销低于6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM、求解器和智能体团队生成的工作流动作、修复和计划可能语法有效但存在过时、不可行、冲突或破坏触发修复的证据等问题，需要一种事务模型来保证生成动作的可靠执行。

Method: 提出Agentic Transaction Processing (ATP)事务模型，将生成动作视为不可信提案，通过声明的可执行约束集C进行确定性准入；在Mnemosyne中实现，包括仅追加的变迁日志、有效状态投影、依赖安全补偿和主动提交记录；采用局部化修复协议（LCRP）进行有界反应式修复。

Result: 在九个伪造测试中拒绝目标违规的同时接受有效工作，投影与验证开销低于6%，局部修复比全局重算少编辑一个数量级的操作。

Conclusion: ATP模型使提交状态的正确性与提案层的胜任力、诚实性或学习能力无关，保证了权威分离、串行等价生成准入、证据保留修复和约束包含四项安全属性，并提供了有界反应式修复保证。

Abstract: LLMs, solvers, and agent teams increasingly generate workflow actions, repairs, and plans, but a generated action may be syntactically valid yet stale, infeasible, conflicting, or destructive of the evidence that triggered a repair. We introduce Agentic Transaction Processing (ATP), a transaction model that treats generated actions as untrusted proposals until they pass deterministic admission under a declared, executable constraint set C. The principle is two-sided: a proposal is not truth, and no proposal foresees every disruption: anything may propose, but only the runtime admits and commits, and when an unforeseen disruption strikes it repairs reactively within bounds rather than trusting a fresh proposal. Relative to C, committed-state correctness becomes independent of the competence, honesty, or learning of the proposing layer. We realize ATP in Mnemosyne, a runtime with an append-only transition log, effective-state projection, dependency-safe compensation, and active commitment records, and prove four safety properties relative to C (authority separation, serial-equivalent generative admission, evidence-preserving repair, and obligation containment) together with a bounded-reactive-repair guarantee for its localized repair protocol (LCRP). A reproducible artifact rejects the targeted violations across nine falsification tests while still admitting valid work, at under 6% projection-and-validation overhead, and bounded local repair edits an order of magnitude fewer operations than global recompute. Mnemosyne is open source: https://github.com/eyuchang/Mnemosyne/tree/arxiv-atp-rq1-rq9b-r8-v2.

</details>


### [239] [Managed Autonomy at Runtime: Gear-Based Safety and Governance for Single- and Multi-Agent Cyber-Physical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00334)
*Srini Ramaswamy,Wang Miaosheng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一个离散时间控制系统\system{}，结合五种执行齿轮（观察、建议、规划、执行、交互）与效用门控调度和事件驱动回退，为单智能体提供单调稳定性、执行安全等理论保证，并为多智能体CPS系统应用\smart{}管理自主生命周期，通过共识门控、群体Lyapunov分析等实现分布式安全与稳定性。在三台UR5机器人装配单元上，基于NIST数据集进行10,000次蒙特卡洛实验，异常检测率达99.6%（基线2.1%），检测延迟降低3.5倍，并提供了形式化的物理工作空间安全证书。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主智能体（无论LLM驱动的软件智能体还是机器人物理智能体）在缺乏持续人工监督时面临三类常见故障模式：未验证动作导致的安全违规、无约束循环导致的行为不稳定性、未处理错误状态导致的连续性丢失。现有系统缺乏统一的理论框架来同时保证安全、稳定和连续性。

Method: 提出\system{}离散时间控制系统，核心结构包括：(1) 五种执行齿轮（观察、建议、规划、执行、交互）作为微级权限；(2) 效用门控调度与事件驱动回退机制；(3) 单智能体方面：证明单调稳定性、执行安全、最终稳定、回退完备性，并等价于齿轮约束MDP；(4) 多智能体CPS方面：应用\smart{}管理自主生命周期（稳定/元/辅助/调节四个治理状态），结合共识门控、群体Lyapunov分析、每智能体齿轮权限和会合控制；(5) 执行齿轮作为\smart{}运行时治理状态下的微级权限，分离动作控制与自主治理。

Result: 在三台UR5机器人装配单元上，使用NIST《机器人手臂位置精度退化测量》数据集校准故障幅度，进行10,000次蒙特卡洛实验。系统达到99.6%的异常检测率（单智能体基线为2.1%），检测延迟降低3.5倍，并提供形式化物理工作空间安全证书。

Conclusion: 该系统通过执行齿轮与治理状态的分层设计，有效解决了自主智能体的安全违规、行为不稳定和连续性丢失问题。理论证明与实验验证共同表明，该方法在单智能体和多智能体CPS场景下均能提供可证明的安全与稳定性保证，且分离了动作控制与自主治理的关注点。

Abstract: Autonomous agents, whether LLM-driven software agents or robotic physical agents, face a common class of failure modes when operating without continuous human oversight: safety violations from unverified actions, behavioral instability from unconstrained loops, and continuity loss from unhandled error states. We develop \system{}, a discrete-time control system that combines five execution gears (\Gobs{}, \Gsug{}, \Gplan{}, \Gexec{}, \Gint{}) with utility-gated dispatch and event-driven fallback. For the single-agent case, we prove monotonic stability, execution safety, eventual stabilization, fallback completeness, and equivalence to a gear-constrained Markov decision process. For multi-agent cyber-physical systems (CPS), we apply the established \smart{} managed-autonomy lifecycle and map runtime evidence into its four governance states (\Stable{}/\Meta{}/\Assisted{}/\Regulated{}). Consensus gating, swarm-level Lyapunov analysis, per-agent gear authority, and rendezvous control provide distributed safety and stability guarantees, including zero collision under the stated assumptions. We evaluate the resulting runtime on a three-agent UR5 robotic assembly cell using fault magnitudes calibrated from the NIST \emph{Degradation Measurement of Robot Arm Position Accuracy} dataset across 10,000 Monte Carlo episodes. It achieves a 99.6\% anomaly detection rate versus 2.1\% for the single-agent baseline, reduces detection latency by $3.5\times$, and supplies a formal physical-workspace safety certificate. The execution gears act as micro-level permissions beneath the \smart{} runtime governance states, separating action control from autonomy governance.

*Tianci Liu,Zihan Dong,Linjun Zhang,Haoyu Wang,jing Gao,Emre Kiciman,Ranveer Chandra,Wei-Ting Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SPIRE是一个基于逆规划的多智能体强化学习框架，通过结构去噪实现页面级幻灯片个性化设计，无需预设模板或工具知识。

Method: 将PSP形式化为逆规划问题，提出SPIRE框架：通过故意破坏干净幻灯片的视觉结构，创建一个可验证的去噪任务，两个智能体通过强化学习协作优化可执行设计。证明了结构去噪是PSP的一致替代目标，且多智能体公式严格降低了RL中的策略梯度方差。

Result: 大量实验证明了SPIRE的优越性能。

Conclusion: SPIRE通过结构去噪和双智能体协作的RL方法，有效解决了页面级幻灯片个性化问题，提供了无需工具先验知识的设计意图学习方案。

Abstract: Slide design requires personalizing both deck themes and page layouts. Yet, current AI agent-based methods struggle with fine-grained, page-level design. Solely relying on prespecified templates or user verbose instructions, they fail to capture latent design intents, leaving Page-level Slide Personalization (PSP) unresolved. To close this gap, this work formulates PSP as an inverse planning problem. We propose to learn a design intent without assuming any knowledge of the specific executing tools (e.g., PowerPoint, Beamer) being used. However, relinquishing control over these tools makes the problem intractable to optimize end-to-end. To overcome this, we propose SPIRE, a principled framework to solve PSP approximately. By intentionally corrupting the visual structures of clean slides, SPIRE creates a verifiable task to denoise the corruption, whereby two agents learn to collaboratively refine executable designs via reinforcement learning (RL). We present a proof that structural denoising is a consistent surrogate for PSP, and that the multi-agent formulation strictly reduces policy gradient variance in RL. Extensive experiments demonstrate the superiority of SPIRE.

### [241] [PHREEQC-MCQ-200: A Diagnostic Benchmark for Tool-Augmented Scientific Simulator Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00436)
*Ke Zhang,Sahchit Chundur,Mohammad Javad Qomi,Maziar Raissi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PHREEQC-MCQ-200基准，用于评估工具增强型智能体在地球化学模拟中的表现。研究发现模拟器访问提升了整体准确率，但非单调：工具增强代理会丢失先前无工具时正确回答的样本。输出访问协议（如目录接口）对强模型有效，但会降低中端模型性能。建议科学工具评估应报告准确率之外的多种细粒度诊断指标。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建PHREEQC-MCQ-200基准，包含200道多选题，源自21个经过验证的PHREEQC场景。要求代理构建模拟器输入、执行PHREEQC、检查结构化输出并提交最终答案。跨多个前沿和中端模型家族进行实验，比较有无工具访问时的性能差异，并测试不同的输出访问协议（如目录接口）。

Result: 模拟器访问显著提升了整体聚合准确率，但增益非单调：工具增强代理会丢失先前无工具时正确回答的样本。目录接口可降低强模型的token成本并保持或提升准确率，但会降低无法可靠导航结构化输出的中端模型性能。

Conclusion: PHREEQC-MCQ-200将科学工具使用视为端到端诊断问题而非简单工具调用能力。评估科学代理时应报告准确率之外的多种指标：项目级保留率、输出访问敏感性、轨迹失败点以及计算链断裂位置。

Abstract: Large language model agents are increasingly connected to scientific software, yet it remains unclear when tool access makes scientific computation more reliable rather than merely more complex. We introduce PHREEQC-MCQ-200, a benchmark for evaluating tool-augmented agents on deterministic aqueous-geochemistry simulations. The benchmark contains 200 multiple-choice questions derived from 21 validated PHREEQC scenarios, requiring agents to construct simulator inputs, execute PHREEQC, inspect structured outputs, and commit to final answers.
  Across multiple frontier and mid-tier model families, simulator access substantially improves aggregate accuracy, confirming that grounded execution is necessary for many scientific-computation tasks. However, the gains are not monotonic: tool-augmented agents also lose items they answered correctly without tools, revealing regressions that average accuracy alone hides. We further show that output-access protocol matters. A table-of-contents interface can reduce token cost while preserving or improving accuracy for stronger models, but it degrades performance for mid-tier models that cannot reliably navigate structured simulator outputs.
  PHREEQC-MCQ-200 therefore frames scientific tool use as an end-to-end diagnostic problem rather than a simple tool-calling capability. We argue that evaluations of scientific agents should report not only accuracy, but also item-level retention, output-access sensitivity, trajectory failures, and where the computation chain breaks.

Abstract: Agricultural advisory systems face a fundamental tension: static agronomic guidelines offer consistent, evidence-based recommendations, yet remain blind to in-season variability and dynamic uncertainties. To assess this framework, we evaluate three reasoning approaches, namely Plan-and-Solve, Tree of Thoughts, and Reflexion, over a 10-year retrospective analysis. All three significantly outperform static PoP (Package-of-Practice) baselines, with Tree of Thoughts achieving impressive peak yields. ### [243] [Multi-scale Mixture of World Models for Embodied Agents in Evolving Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00457)

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MuSix通过尺度感知的世界模型混合与进化框架，解决了具身智能体在现实世界中多尺度推理和知识适应的两个关键挑战：路由缺乏显式尺度概念，以及统一更新策略无法适应不同尺度知识的不同过时速率。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出MuSix框架，包含两阶段路由机制：元路由首先将体验距离（受CLT启发的情境新颖性度量）映射到连续尺度空间的权重，然后每个尺度的基路由器选择该尺度内的世界模型。适应方面采用尺度依赖的遗忘率，低尺度知识快速更新而高尺度抽象持久保留，并通过门控跨尺度传输维持层级一致性。

Result: 在EmbodiedBench和HAZARD基准上，MuSix在多尺度推理和动态适应方面优于最先进的基线方法。

Conclusion: MuSix通过尺度感知的路由和差异化的更新策略，有效解决了具身智能体中多尺度知识混合与适应的问题。

Abstract: Embodied agents operating in the real world require multi-scale reasoning and knowledge adaptation as conditions change. We identify two challenges in applying Mixture of Experts (MoE) to this setting: routing lacks an explicit notion of scale, preventing targeted updates at specific scales, and a uniform update policy cannot accommodate the different rates at which knowledge at each scale becomes outdated. We present MuSix, a framework that addresses both challenges through scale-aware world model mixture and evolution. A two-stage routing mechanism grounds scale selection in experiential distance, a measure of situational novelty inspired by Construal Level Theory: a meta-router first maps this quantity to a weight over continuous scale space, then per-scale base routers select world models within the identified scale. For adaptation, scale-dependent forgetting rates allow low-scale knowledge to refresh rapidly while high-scale abstractions persist, and gated inter-scale transfer maintains coherence across the hierarchy. Experiments on EmbodiedBench and HAZARD show that MuSix improves over state-of-the-art baselines on multi-scale reasoning and dynamic adaptation.

This counterfactual criterion separates AI-native games from AI-augmented games, boundary artifacts, chatbots, tavern-style role-play, procedural content generation, and AI-assisted production. We argue that the central design problem is organizing semantic openness into stable gameplay. AI-native design depends on mechanical invariants: goals, rules, state, feedback, pacing, and player agency that make open-ended AI outputs interpretable and consequential. ### [245] [HARC: Coupling Harmfulness and Refusal Directions for Robust Safety Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00572)
*Shei Pern Chua,Fangzhao Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文发现对齐LLM中，有害性和拒绝方向在残差流中可分离，越狱通过抑制这些方向实现。基于此提出HARC微调方法，通过耦合提示和响应位置的两个方向来增强安全鲁棒性，且不损害通用能力。HARC在六个基线中实现了最优的鲁棒性-能力-可用性权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解对齐LLM内部如何表征安全性对于诊断对齐漏洞至关重要，因为它能解释越狱为何成功，并为设计稳健的对齐策略提供依据。

Method: 提出了HARC（Harmfulness-And-Refusal Coupling）微调方法，将有害性和拒绝方向在提示和响应位置进行耦合，且干预仅局限于有害性-拒绝子空间，不破坏残差流其余部分。

Result: HARC在跨五个模型家族和两个规模的实验中，在六个基线方法中实现了最强的鲁棒性-能力-可用性权衡，且有害性和拒绝方向可在模型间迁移而无需架构特定调参。

Conclusion: 对齐LLM在生成响应时能识别自身产生的内容是否为有害（即使提示阶段未识别出），越狱通过抑制拒绝/有害方向实现；HARC通过耦合两个方向在不同位置进行微调，可有效提升安全鲁棒性且不牺牲通用能力。

Abstract: Understanding how aligned LLMs internally represent safety is critical for diagnosing alignment vulnerabilities, as it explains why jailbreaks succeed and informs the design of robust alignment strategies. Prior work shows that aligned LLMs encode harmfulness and refusal as separable directions in the residual stream at prompt-side token positions. We show that jailbreaks succeed at prompt encoding by suppressing either the refusal or harmfulness direction before any token is generated, with distinct attack classes occupying separable regions of the harmfulness-refusal plane. Extending the analysis to response-token positions, we find that the model recognizes harmful content while it is generating that content, even when it failed to recognize the input as harmful at the prompt side. Motivated by our findings, we introduce HARC (Harmfulness-And-Refusal Coupling), a fine-tuning method that pairs the two directions across both prompt and response positions. Since the intervention is confined to the harmfulness-refusal subspace, it leaves the rest of the residual stream intact and does not degrade general capability or inflate over-refusal. Across extensive experiments, HARC achieves the strongest robustness-capability-usability trade-off among six baselines spanning the major training-time and inference-time safety methods. The harmfulness and refusal directions at prompt and response positions transfer across the five model families and two scales we tested without architecture-specific tuning.

### [246] [AGI Maze as a Benchmark Framework for World-Modeling Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00627)

TL;DR: 本文提出了AGI Maze框架，用于构建需要智能体学习并使用世界状态表征的网格迷宫任务。实验表明，普通LLM在推理时无法内部表征迷宫，即使允许使用消息历史作为工作记忆，LLM智能体在步数预算充足的情况下仍无法可靠解决小规模迷宫。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are powerful pattern-completion systems, but their default operating mode - predicting the next token from a static context - does not reliably produce persistent, manipulable representations of an external world. Many tasks that look like "reasoning" in text become substantially harder once the environment is partially observable, stateful, and requires memory and structured hypotheses about hidden state. AGI Maze is a lightweight framework for building such environments without requiring high-dimensional sensory inputs. It provides a family of grid-based maze tasks with a clean API and multiple difficulty regimes. The goal is to create benchmarks where agents must learn and use world state representations, not just infer a local rule over readily provided observations. We provide an initial evaluation of several vanilla LLMs on simple mazes showing that they fail to represent mazes internally at LLM inference time. We also introduce a baseline agent, which is allowed to use its message history as a working memory to construct descriptions of observations at agentic runtime. Although this can improve performance, it is still insufficient for an LLM agent to reliably solve even small mazes within a step budget that is more than enough for humans.

### [247] [Coachable agents for interactive gameplay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00642)

However, there are many use cases in which one would like to assert some level of control, preferably in real time, over how the task is solved. We refer to these modifications of a core task as styles. We combine universal value function approximators (UVFAs) with carefully selected training scenarios, learning algorithms, and data augmentation to create a framework for coaching agents that exhibit styles in complex domains. We demonstrate the framework's application in the AAA video games Horizon Forbidden West and Gran Turismo, and in an open-source humanoid test domain. Despite the different nature of the domains -- car racing, stylized game combat, and humanoid walking -- each agent shows strong coherence to the style requests while still satisfying the main task in its domain. ### [248] [Self-GC: Self-Governing Context for Long-Horizon LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00692)
*Xubin Hao,Hongjin Meng,Xin Yin,Jiawei Zhu,Chenpeng Cao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出Self-GC，一种面向长上下文LLM代理的上下文管理系统，将上下文对象索引化并通过侧通道规划器执行折叠、掩码和剪枝操作，而非简单的文本清理。在多项实验中将无影响率提升至91-95%，远超启发式基线的55-87%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文LLM代理累积的工具结果、文件、计划和用户约束具有高度结构化特征，现有基于启发式（时序剪枝、工具输出掩码）或最终自我摘要的方法无法有效管理：启发式方法忽略未来依赖，摘要方法丢失精确证据和可编辑工件。亟需一种将上下文管理视为运行时生命周期控制的方法。

Method: Self-GC将用户轮次、工具片段和技能状态转化为索引化对象；引入侧通道规划器提出折叠（fold）、掩码（mask）和剪枝（prune）动作；由执行框架实现可恢复的侧车（sidecar）、安全提交边界和缓存感知提交策略。

Result: 在33会话Hard Set上，剪枝43.95%前缀token，84.85%未来延续不受影响（基线无影响率54.55%-69.70%）；在332会话生产级数据集上，三个规划器骨干达到91.27%-94.58%无影响率（基线77.71%-87.46%）；在线账户级拆分使日间平均输入token减少10%-15%，峰值接近20%。

Conclusion: 上下文管理应被视作对索引化、可恢复对象的运行时生命周期控制，而非事后文本清理。

Abstract: Long-horizon LLM agents accumulate tool results, files, plans, and user constraints that are too structured to be treated as a disposable text suffix. Current systems mostly rely on in-run heuristics such as chronological pruning and tool-output masking, or on final self-summary near a context limit. Heuristics are cheap but blind to future dependencies; summaries preserve narrative state but often hide exact evidence, locators, and editable artifacts. We present Self-GC, where GC denotes self-governing context while deliberately echoing garbage collection: the system does not merely reclaim unused tokens, but governs the lifecycle of agent context objects. Self-GC turns user turns, tool spans, and skill state into indexed objects; asks a side-channel planner to propose fold, mask, and prune actions; and lets the harness enforce recoverable sidecars, safe commit boundaries, and cache-aware commit. On a 33-session Hard Set, Self-GC prunes 43.95% of prefix tokens while leaving 84.85% of future continuations unaffected, compared with no-impact rates of 54.55% to 69.70% for heuristic baselines. On a 332-session production-derived suite, three planner backbones reach no-impact rates of 91.27% to 94.58%, while baselines remain at 77.71% to 87.46%. In production, an online account-level split reduces daytime average input tokens by 10% to 15%, with peak reductions near 20%. These results point to context management as runtime lifecycle control over indexed, recoverable objects rather than post hoc text cleanup.

</details>


### [249] [Self-Evolving Agents with Anytime-Valid Certificates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00871)
*Biswa Sengupta*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SEA是一种将自我修改限制在小型转向适配器和版本化框架内的架构，通过随时有效的门控机制（带固定错误预算的可审计证书）来控制修改，利用五个循环控制器和五个验证器在环机制，在冻结基础模型上仅选择已有行为，在SWE-bench验证集上实现了性能提升且防止了回归。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自我进化代理违背了大多数学习理论保障的假设：数据、评估器、组件和假设空间都是由正在更新的策略产生的。这导致传统理论保证不再适用，需要新的架构来安全地实现自我修改。

Method: 提出SEA架构：(1) 将自我修改限制在小型转向适配器和版本化框架内；(2) 冻结基础模型；(3) 通过随时有效的门控机制（带固定错误预算的可审计证书）控制每次修改；(4) 五个循环控制器组合已有保证；(5) 五种验证器在环机制（最佳N、微步搜索、自创再现神谕、搜索层控制、自我修复）提供门控所需的密集无评分信号。

Result: 在52个实例的SWE-bench验证集上，跨四个基础模型，基础能力是主导效应。在两个强基础模型上，无操作组合控制隔离出+4和+5的提升（GLM 5.2: 24→28；GPT: 29→34，最佳65%），事件日志确认机制触发并防止了回归。

Conclusion: SEA架构能安全地实现自我进化代理，在冻结基础模型上通过可控的门控机制和验证器在环机制提升性能并防止回归。结果是单次运行的昂贵评估，确认运行间方差和调整每任务算法组合是未来工作。

Abstract: Self-evolving agents violate the assumption behind most learning-theoretic guarantees: the data, evaluator, components, and hypothesis space are produced by the policy being updated. We present \textbf{SEA}, an architecture that confines self-modification to a small steering adapter and a versioned harness around a \emph{frozen} base model and admits each modification only through an anytime-valid gate that emits an auditable certificate against a fixed error budget. Five loop controllers compose published guarantees; because such gates can only \emph{select} among behaviors the frozen base already produces, five verifier-in-the-loop mechanisms -- best-of-$N$, micro-step search, self-authored reproduction oracles, search-layer control, and self-repair -- supply the dense, grader-free signal the gates require, computed from the issue text alone. On a $52$-instance SWE-bench Verified subset across four base models, base capability is the dominant, confound-free effect, and on two strong base models a deliberate no-op-composite control isolates the suite's contribution at $+4$ and $+5$ (\textsc{Glm}~5.2 $24\to28$; \textsc{Gpt} $29\to34$, the $65\%$ best), with event logs confirming that its mechanisms fire and prevent regressions. Results are single-run on expensive evaluations; confirming run-to-run variance and adapting the per-task algorithm mix are future work.

</details>


### [250] [Two AI Metrics Diverged: Will it Make All the Difference?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00913)
*Alex Fogelson,Zachary A. Brown,Hans Gundlach,Jayson Lynch,Neil Thompson*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了随着AI模型计算规模指数级增长，前沿模型的能力是否会超越小预算开发者所能触及的范围，还是能力会趋于收敛、让小模型“继承地球”。研究表明答案取决于如何衡量AI能力：验证损失显示差距缩小，但其他指标上前沿模型领先优势持续扩大。通过将性能指标按与计算量的函数关系分类，给出了决定哪些指标有利于小模型的严格数学条件，并指出有界指标始终有利于小模型。但许多常见有界指标存在对应的无界指标，仔细解读至关重要——有界与无界指标可能指向相反的政策建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在计算规模指数增长的背景下，前沿AI模型的能力是否会与小预算开发者可及的能力趋同，以及这一问题的答案如何依赖于能力度量方式的选择。

Method: 基于Gundlach等人(2025b)的工作，将性能指标按与训练（及推理）计算量的函数关系进行分类，推导出判断哪些指标有利于“温和模型”（小模型）的严格数学条件，并分析有界与无界指标的对偶关系。

Result: 验证损失显示前沿模型与小模型差距缩小，但在其他指标上前沿模型领先优势持续扩大；有界性能指标始终有利于小模型；许多常见有界指标存在对应的无界指标（反之亦然）。

Conclusion: 对于特定能力（如软件工程、合成生物学、修辞说服力），若其有意义的度量方式是无界的，则前沿能力将集中在少数富裕行为者手中；若是有界的，则前沿能力将通过小模型普及到大众手中。正确的度量选择是政策制定的前提。

Abstract: As exponential compute scaling continues, will the capabilities of frontier AI models outstrip what is accessible to developers on a small fixed budget? Or will capabilities converge, with "meek models inheriting the earth"? Building on Gundlach et al. (2025b), we show that the answer depends on how we value and measure AI capabilities. We discuss conventional performance measures and show that, while validation loss shows a shrinking gap, on other metrics frontier models grow their lead forever. Classifying performance metrics by their functional forms in relation to training (and inference) compute, we provide tight mathematical conditions for determining which metrics favor meek models, and show that bounded performance metrics always do. But careful interpretation of performance metrics is essential: we show that many common bounded metrics have closely-related counterpart metrics that are unbounded (and vice versa). Determining the apt metric in a domain is a prerequisite for policy, since bounded and unbounded metrics may suggest opposing policy responses. If a particular capability -- like software engineering, synthetic biology, or rhetorical persuasiveness -- is unbounded when measured in the terms we care about, frontier-level capability will likely be concentrated in the hands of a few wealthy actors. Conversely, if that capability is instead bounded, frontier-level capabilities proliferate through meek models into the hands of the many.

</details>

Method: 开发Graph-PRefLexOR图原生推理模型系列，采用Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO)进行微调，将推理过程组织为机制探索、图构建、模式提取和假设合成四个显式阶段，将神经语言生成与符号关系结构相链接，实现因果关系的构建、检查和复用。

Standard large language models often produce fluent but weakly traceable responses to open-ended materials design problems, making it difficult to determine whether final answers are supported by coherent intermediate reasoning. We develop Graph-PRefLexOR, a family of graph-native reasoning models fine-tuned with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to organize reasoning into explicit phases for mechanism exploration, graph construction, pattern extraction, and hypothesis synthesis. This design links neural language generation with symbolic relational structure, enabling causal connections to be constructed, inspected, and reused. On 100 open-ended questions from materials science and mechanics literature, Graph-PRefLexOR achieves 40-65% improvements over corresponding base models, with the largest gains in reasoning traceability. Embedding analyses show broader semantic exploration and approximately 2-3 times greater semantic diversity than baselines. Semantic backtracking and layer-wise hidden-state analyses further show stronger alignment between structured reasoning and final answers. Finally, test-time graph expansion reveals that additional compute primarily increases long-range conceptual recombination within a bounded semantic space, rather than simply expanding semantic coverage. These results establish graph-native reinforcement learning as a pathway toward interpretable AI systems for scientific hypothesis generation in materials design and other scientific applications.

  <summary>Details</summary>

These signals are propagated through a Bayesian Network (BN) to estimate system-level uncertainty and provide node-level indicators of potential failure points across the workflow. The approach is evaluated on StrategyQA and HotpotQA using GPT-3.5-Turbo and GPT-4.1-Nano, with Area Under the Receiver Operating Characteristic Curve (AUROC), Area Under the Accuracy-Rejection Curve (AUARC), Expected Calibration Error (ECE), and Brier Score used to assess discrimination, selective prediction and calibration. Results show that Bayesian propagation is more effective on HotpotQA, where uncertainty accumulates across multi-hop reasoning stages, while StrategyQA exposes limitations caused by miscalibration and unreliable upstream signals. This paper presents PedNStream (Pedestrian Network Flow Simulation), an open-source, Python-native simulator for macroscopic pedestrian network loading based on the Link Transmission Model (LTM). PedNStream is implemented as a modular framework with built-in controller interfaces for interventions such as gating, flow separation, and route guidance. We evaluate the framework in a staged manner. Synthetic scenarios verify key mechanisms, including queue formation, spillback, congestion dissipation, and adaptive rerouting. Real-network experiments assess large-scale behavior and consistency with observed pedestrian counts. ### [254] [Agentic generation of verifiable rules for deterministic, self-expanding reaction classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01061)

Abstract: Computer-assisted synthesis planning breaks target molecules into accessible precursors using large libraries of reaction rules that assign each transformation a deterministic, interpretable label. But chemistry is long-tailed, making manual encoding intractable, and existing tools rely on fixed rulesets that cannot adapt to new chemistries. Here we present a fully automated pipeline in which a multi-agent framework of large language models (LLMs) classifies reactions and writes the rules themselves across 665,901 US patent reactions, generating each rule under a verification loop that tests it against the corpus. It expands a standard taxonomy from 68 to 14,073 classes without human curation. With a lightweight fingerprint classifier, it classifies 97.7\% of unseen reactions, matching a leading proprietary classifier while resolving chemistry more finely and extending on demand to chemistry outside its training distribution. The result is a living reactivity database and a general route to turning generative models into reliable, self-expanding symbolic systems.

</details>


### [255] [Can Agents Generalize to the Open World? Unveiling the Fragility of Static Training in Tool Use](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01084)
*Song-Lin Lv,Weiming Wu,Rui Zhu,Zi-Jian Cheng,Lan-Zhe Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了OpenAgent问题设置，定义了查询、动作、观察和领域四个维度的分布偏移，构建了包含四层层次（感知、交互、推理、内化）的受控沙箱环境，系统分析了SFT和RL训练的LLM Agent在开放环境下的性能退化，并提出了扰动增强微调（Perturbation-Augmented Fine-Tuning）作为提升鲁棒性的干预策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM Agent在静态基准上表现良好，但在真实部署中面临用户查询、工具集和交互动态的不断变化，存在显著的泛化差距。本文旨在形式化并系统诊断这一开放环境下的泛化问题。

Method: 形式化了OpenAgent问题设置；构建了受控沙箱环境，定义四层层次（感知、交互、推理、内化）的细粒度环境偏移；提出了Perturbation-Augmented Fine-Tuning（扰动增强微调）作为SFT阶段的干预策略。

Result: 实验表明，无论是SFT还是RL训练的Agent在面对开放环境偏移时都会出现不同程度的性能退化。

Conclusion: 扰动增强微调策略能够为提升Agent在真实环境中的鲁棒性和实用性奠定基础。

Abstract: While Large Language Model (LLM) agents demonstrate proficiency in static benchmarks, their deployment in real-world scenarios is hindered by the dynamic nature of user queries, tool sets, and interaction dynamics. To address this generalization gap, we formalize OpenAgent (Tool-Use Agent in Open-World), a problem setting characterized by distributional shifts across query, action, observation, and domain dimensions. To systematically diagnose its impact, we construct a controlled sandbox environment where we define fine-grained environmental shifts across a four-tier hierarchy, Perception, Interaction, Reasoning, and Internalization, and conduct a comprehensive series of experiments. Our analysis yields a series of key insights, demonstrating that agents trained via both Supervised Fine-Tuning(SFT) and Reinforcement Learning suffer from varying degrees of performance degradation when confronting open environmental shifts. Building on these insights, we propose Perturbation-Augmented Fine-Tuning, a disturbance-based intervention strategy for SFT that lays the foundation for enhancing agent robustness and utility in realistic environments. Our code will be released at: https://github. com/LAMDA-NeSy/OpenAgent.
